<p><b>Mauro Emanuel Icardi</b>  (<small>Spanish pronunciation:&#160;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Spanish" title="Help:IPA/Spanish">[mawo emanwel ikaði]</a></span>; born 19 February 1993) is an Argentine professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Striker_(association_football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Striker (association football)">striker</a> for <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> club <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina national team</a>.
</p><p>Icardi began his footballing career at <a href="/wiki/La_Masia" title="La Masia">La Masia</a>, the youth system of <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> club <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a>, before moving to <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> club <a href="/wiki/U.C._Sampdoria" title="U.C. Sampdoria">Sampdoria</a> to begin his professional career in 2012; after an impressive season, he joined <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Inter Milan</a>  in July 2013,<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> where he developed into one of the most prolific strikers in Europe. Icardi won the <i><a href="/wiki/Capocannoniere" title="Capocannoniere">Capocannoniere</a></i> in both the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Serie_A" title="2014–15 Serie A">2014–15</a> and <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Serie_A" title="2017–18 Serie A">2017–18</a> seasons,<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;a&#93;</a></sup> and was named the captain of Inter in 2015, at age 22.<sup id="cite_ref-:2_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-5">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> Three years later, Icardi was integral for Inter reaching a place in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a>, their first time in six years,<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> as he became the club's <a href="/wiki/List_of_Inter_Milan_records_and_statistics" title="List of Inter Milan records and statistics">eighth highest goalscorer of all time</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> In 2019, Icardi signed for Paris Saint-Germain on an initial one-year loan deal,<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> where he won a domestic treble. He then joined the club permanentely in a €50 million deal.
</p><p>Icardi made his senior debut for <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a> in October 2013 but since has played sparingly. Icardi was controversially left out of Argentina's final squad for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-:3_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:3-9">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Icardi has been a subject of controversy due to his marriage to <a href="/wiki/Wanda_Nara" title="Wanda Nara">Wanda Nara</a>, whose ex-husband is Icardi's former Sampdoria teammate <a href="/wiki/Maxi_L%C3%B3pez" title="Maxi López">Maxi López</a>. López and Nara divorced because of her exposed relationship with Icardi.<sup id="cite_ref-:4_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:4-10">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career">Early career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Icardi was born in <a href="/wiki/Rosario,_Santa_Fe" title="Rosario, Santa Fe">Rosario</a>, Argentina and moved to <a href="/wiki/Canary_Islands" title="Canary Islands">Canary Islands</a> when he was nine. He began his football career with <a href="/wiki/UD_Vecindario" title="UD Vecindario">Vecindario</a> in <a href="/wiki/Gran_Canaria" title="Gran Canaria">Gran Canaria</a>, and scored over 50 goals in their youth categories.
</p><p>In 2007, he was disputed over by <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> and <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." class="mw-redirect" title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a>, after offers from <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a>, <a href="/wiki/RCD_Espanyol" title="RCD Espanyol">Espanyol</a>, <a href="/wiki/Deportivo_de_La_Coru%C3%B1a" title="Deportivo de La Coruña">Deportivo La Coruña</a>, <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> and <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a>. Barcelona won the race for Icardi, and signed with him until 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Icardi joined the Catalan club at the start of <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_FC_Barcelona_season" title="2008–09 FC Barcelona season">2008–09 season</a> and was included on the U-17 team. He was promoted to the <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona_Juvenil_A" class="mw-redirect" title="FC Barcelona Juvenil A">U-19 team</a> the following season before joining <a href="/wiki/U.C._Sampdoria" title="U.C. Sampdoria">Sampdoria</a> on loan in January 2011. Icardi later stated that leaving Barcelona was not a bad decision, convinced that his decision to move on was the right one.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sampdoria">Sampdoria</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Sampdoria">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:MauroIcardi.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/MauroIcardi.jpg/170px-MauroIcardi.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="186" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/MauroIcardi.jpg/255px-MauroIcardi.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ef/MauroIcardi.jpg/340px-MauroIcardi.jpg 2x" data-file-width="369" data-file-height="403" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:MauroIcardi.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Icardi in <a href="/wiki/U.C._Sampdoria" title="U.C. Sampdoria">Sampdoria</a> colours, 2011</div></div></div>
<p>On 11 January 2011, Sampdoria confirmed Icardi had signed with the club on loan<sup id="cite_ref-a_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-a-13">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> until the end of the season. After a successful six-month loan for <i>la Samp</i>, scoring 13 goals in 19 games with the Primavera team, the Italian side utilised the option to buy Icardi for €400,000 in July 2011, signing a three-year deal.<sup id="cite_ref-a_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-a-13">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> In 2011–12 season, he scored 19 goals in the reserve league Group A, as the joint-third topscorer of the league along with <a href="/wiki/Gonzalo_Barreto" title="Gonzalo Barreto">Gonzalo Barreto</a> of Group C.
</p><p>On 12 May 2012, he made his first-team debut, against <a href="/wiki/S.S._Juve_Stabia" title="S.S. Juve Stabia">Juve Stabia</a>, after coming off the bench to replace <a href="/wiki/Bruno_Fornaroli" title="Bruno Fornaroli">Bruno Fornaroli</a> in the 75th minute of the match. Ten minutes later, Icardi scored his first professional goal to win the match 2–1 for Sampdoria.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 26 September 2012, he made his <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> debut for Sampdoria against <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">Roma</a>, substituting the Paraguayan midfielder <a href="/wiki/Marcelo_Estigarribia" title="Marcelo Estigarribia">Marcelo Estigarribia</a> in the 49th minute.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> On 12 November, Icardi scored his first goal in Serie A in the <a href="/wiki/Derby_della_Lanterna" title="Derby della Lanterna">Derby della Lanterna</a> against <a href="/wiki/Genoa_C.F.C." title="Genoa C.F.C.">Genoa</a> in an eventual 3–1 win.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> On 6 January 2013, he scored two goals against <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> in Sampdoria's 2–1 upset at <a href="/wiki/Juventus_Stadium" title="Juventus Stadium">Juventus Stadium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> It was Juventus's second ever loss in the Juventus Stadium since the construction.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 27 January 2013, he scored four goals in a six-goal thrashing of fellow strugglers <a href="/wiki/Delfino_Pescara_1936" title="Delfino Pescara 1936">Pescara</a>, lifting the <a href="/wiki/Genoa" title="Genoa">Genoese</a> side clear of the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Serie_A" title="2012–13 Serie A">Serie A</a> relegation zone.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> On 18 May, during the final match of <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Serie_A" title="2012–13 Serie A">2012–13 season</a>, Icardi scored again against Juventus, helping the team to beat the eventual champions of Italy 3–2 at <a href="/wiki/Stadio_Luigi_Ferraris" title="Stadio Luigi Ferraris">Stadio Luigi Ferraris</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Inter_Milan">Inter Milan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Inter Milan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Avropa_Liqas%C4%B1_Muzeyi_Bak%C4%B1da_11.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Avropa_Liqas%C4%B1_Muzeyi_Bak%C4%B1da_11.jpg/170px-Avropa_Liqas%C4%B1_Muzeyi_Bak%C4%B1da_11.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="224" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Avropa_Liqas%C4%B1_Muzeyi_Bak%C4%B1da_11.jpg/255px-Avropa_Liqas%C4%B1_Muzeyi_Bak%C4%B1da_11.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Avropa_Liqas%C4%B1_Muzeyi_Bak%C4%B1da_11.jpg/340px-Avropa_Liqas%C4%B1_Muzeyi_Bak%C4%B1da_11.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1872" data-file-height="2470" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Avropa_Liqas%C4%B1_Muzeyi_Bak%C4%B1da_11.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Icardi's <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Inter Milan</a> shirt</div></div></div>
<p>In late April, it was announced that Icardi would join <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Inter Milan</a> before the beginning of the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Serie_A" title="2013–14 Serie A">2013–14 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> The deal was also later confirmed by Sampdoria board.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> The transfer fee was €6.5 million for 50% registration rights.<sup id="cite_ref-Inter2014bilancio_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Inter2014bilancio-24">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Icardi was officially unveiled as an Inter player on 16 July along with Algerian striker <a href="/wiki/Ishak_Belfodil" title="Ishak Belfodil">Ishak Belfodil</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> where he was allocated squad number 9.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPN_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPN-26">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> He said that moving to Inter is a "dream come true",<sup id="cite_ref-ESPN_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPN-26">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> adding that he "had a lot of offers, but wanted only Inter".<sup id="cite_ref-ESPN_FC_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPN_FC-27">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He made his unofficial debut one day later during the 3–0 away win against <a href="/wiki/Trentino" title="Trentino">Trentino</a> Select XI by playing in the first half of the 3–0 away win.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first goal for Inter in their 1–1 pre-season <a href="/wiki/Exhibition_match" class="mw-redirect" title="Exhibition match">friendly</a> draw with <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> club <a href="/wiki/Hamburger_SV" title="Hamburger SV">Hamburger SV</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> netting after less than two minutes on the field and being assisted by <a href="/wiki/Fredy_Guar%C3%ADn" title="Fredy Guarín">Fredy Guarín</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2013.E2.80.9315:_Debut_season_and_Capocannoniere"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2013–15:_Debut_season_and_Capocannoniere">2013–15: Debut season and <i>Capocannoniere</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 2013–15: Debut season and Capocannoniere">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 25 August 2013, Icardi made his Inter official debut, coming on as a second-half <a href="/wiki/Substitute_(association_football)" title="Substitute (association football)">substitute</a> in a 2–0 home success over <a href="/wiki/Genoa_C.F.C." title="Genoa C.F.C.">Genoa</a>, hitting the crossbar late in the game;<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> he scored his first league goal for the <i>Nerazzurri</i> on 14 September, netting the first of a 1–1 home draw against <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a>, after coming on as a substitute in the 73rd minute.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to injury, Icardi missed most of the games of the first part of the season,<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> only returning to first-team matches in February. On 14 February 2014, during the away match against <a href="/wiki/ACF_Fiorentina" title="ACF Fiorentina">Fiorentina</a> at <a href="/wiki/Stadio_Artemio_Franchi" title="Stadio Artemio Franchi">Stadio Artemio Franchi</a>, Icardi returned in the field after four months and scored the winner after only ten minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Later, on 5 April, Icardi scored a brace during the 2–2 home draw against <a href="/wiki/Bologna_F.C._1909" title="Bologna F.C. 1909">Bologna</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> That was his first brace of his Inter career. This was followed by another brace during the 0–4 away win against his former side <a href="/wiki/U.C._Sampdoria" title="U.C. Sampdoria">Sampdoria</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Before the match, he was booed by the home fans, but he quieted them down by scoring in the 13th minute from a cross from <a href="/wiki/Rodrigo_Palacio" title="Rodrigo Palacio">Palacio</a>, making a negative gesture which saw him booked.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 10 May 2014, in <a href="/wiki/Javier_Zanetti" title="Javier Zanetti">Javier Zanetti</a>'s last competitive match at the <a href="/wiki/San_Siro" title="San Siro">San Siro</a>, in which Inter defeated <a href="/wiki/S.S._Lazio" title="S.S. Lazio">Lazio</a> 4–1 to secure a place in <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_UEFA_Europa_League" title="2014–15 UEFA Europa League">Europa League</a> play-off for next season, Icardi scored the second goal of the match in the 37th minute after an assist from <a href="/wiki/Mateo_Kova%C4%8Di%C4%87" title="Mateo Kovai">Kovai</a> and went to celebrate with Zanetti.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> He ended his first season with <i>Nerazzurri</i> with 23 matches in all competitions, including 22 in the league, scoring 9 goals in the process with an average of one goal in every 145 minutes.
</p><p>On 10 June 2014, Inter and Sampdoria reached the deal to terminate the co-ownership for another €6.5 million,<sup id="cite_ref-Inter2014bilancio_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Inter2014bilancio-24">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> making Inter was the sole employer of Icardi in the football field.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Dnepr-Inter_(2).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Dnepr-Inter_%282%29.jpg/170px-Dnepr-Inter_%282%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="362" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/37/Dnepr-Inter_%282%29.jpg 1.5x" data-file-width="233" data-file-height="496" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Dnepr-Inter_(2).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Icardi playing for <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Inter Milan</a> in 2014</div></div></div>
<p>On 20 August 2014, in Inter's first match of <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Inter_Milan_season" title="2014–15 Inter Milan season">the season</a> against Iceland's <a href="/wiki/Stjarnan" title="Stjarnan">Stjarnan</a> for first leg of play-off round of the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_UEFA_Europa_League" title="2014–15 UEFA Europa League">2014–15 Europa League</a>, Icardi opened a 3–0 away win.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> That was his first European goal, in his European debut. In the returning leg, he came in as a second-half substitute and scored two times in a 6–0 win at the <a href="/wiki/San_Siro" title="San Siro">San Siro</a>, to advance his team into the group stage 9–0 on aggregate.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>During the second match of the league season on 14 September, he scored his second <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> hat-trick in a 7–0 thrashing of <a href="/wiki/U.S._Sassuolo_Calcio" title="U.S. Sassuolo Calcio">Sassuolo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Ten days later, Icardi was injured and substituted in the 24th minute for <a href="/wiki/Dani_Osvaldo" title="Dani Osvaldo">Dani Osvaldo</a> during the 2–0 home win against <a href="/wiki/Atalanta_B.C." title="Atalanta B.C.">Atalanta</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> On 26 October, Icardi netted his first Serie A goal for over a month, the winner on a penalty kick against <a href="/wiki/A.C._Cesena" title="A.C. Cesena">Cesena</a> and giving Inter their first away win of the league.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> He was decisive again three days later, scoring a 90th-minute penalty kick won by <a href="/wiki/Zdravko_Kuzmanovi%C4%87" title="Zdravko Kuzmanovi">Zdravko Kuzmanovi</a> in a 1–0 win against <a href="/wiki/U.C._Sampdoria" title="U.C. Sampdoria">Sampdoria</a>, giving his former side their first loss of 2014–15 season.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 9 November, Icardi scored twice after two assists by Palacio during a 2–2 home draw against <a href="/wiki/Hellas_Verona_F.C." title="Hellas Verona F.C.">Hellas Verona</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> This draw caused the sacking of coach <a href="/wiki/Walter_Mazzarri" title="Walter Mazzarri">Walter Mazzarri</a>, who was replaced with the returning <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Mancini" title="Roberto Mancini">Roberto Mancini</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> On 6 January of the following year, in the first match of the second part of the season, Icardi netted the only goal for his team during the 1–1 draw against <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> at <a href="/wiki/Juventus_Stadium" title="Juventus Stadium">Juventus Stadium</a>; the goal came in 64th minute after a pass from the Colombian midfielder <a href="/wiki/Fredy_Guar%C3%ADn" title="Fredy Guarín">Fredy Guarín</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> During that match, he had a conflict with his strike partner Osvaldo who was angry with him after Icardi decided to shoot instead of passing to his teammate who was in a better position to score.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Due to this, Osvaldo left the team in the end of January.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> Five days later, Icardi was decisive in Inter's 3–1 home win against <a href="/wiki/Genoa_C.F.C." title="Genoa C.F.C.">Genoa</a>, scoring the second goal and earlier making an overhead kick (saved by goalkeeper) which was turned into an assist for Palacio.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the match against Sassuolo, Inter lost 1–3 with Icardi scoring the only goal for his team after a mistake from the Sassuolo defence. After the match, he along with Guarín had a conflict with the fans at the <a href="/wiki/Mapei_Stadium" class="mw-redirect" title="Mapei Stadium">Mapei Stadium</a>. They went to throw their shirt to the fans who refused and threw them back at them, spewing insults at them.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> On 7 February, Icardi responded by scoring twice in a 3–0 home win against <a href="/wiki/U.S._Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Città di Palermo">Palermo</a>, refusing to celebrate in the process.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> After the match Icardi told to the media that the reason he did not celebrate was not the conflict with the fans but failing to find a way to renew his contract with the club directors. He was later criticized by Mancini for not celebrating.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 11 April, he scored the first goal during the 0–3 away win against Verona, helping Inter get their first win after six consecutive matches.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> He scored twice on the final day in a 4–3 win over <a href="/wiki/Empoli_F.C." title="Empoli F.C.">Empoli</a> and finished the season as the joint <a href="/wiki/Capocannoniere" title="Capocannoniere">Serie A top goalscorer</a> with 22 goals with Verona's <a href="/wiki/Luca_Toni" title="Luca Toni">Luca Toni</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-top_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-top-54">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Although Inter failed to qualify for European competition for the second time since 1999, Icardi's form attracted attention from abroad, however he signed a new four-year contract at the season's end.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9317:_Captaincy_and_controversy"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015–17:_Captaincy_and_controversy">2015–17: Captaincy and controversy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 2015–17: Captaincy and controversy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Before the start of <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Inter_Milan_season" title="2015–16 Inter Milan season">2015–16 season</a>, it was announced that Icardi would be the new captain of Inter, replacing <a href="/wiki/Andrea_Ranocchia" title="Andrea Ranocchia">Andrea Ranocchia</a> who lost his status after a poor 2014–15 season.<sup id="cite_ref-:2_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-5">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> In his first match as skipper, he was taken off after 15 minutes during the league win against <a href="/wiki/Atalanta_B.C." title="Atalanta B.C.">Atalanta</a>; Icardi was substituted for <a href="/wiki/Stevan_Joveti%C4%87" title="Stevan Joveti">Stevan Joveti</a>, who scored the winning goal in the third minute of added time.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> After the examinations, it was announced that Icardi suffered a thigh injury and he missed the following league match against <a href="/wiki/Carpi_F.C._1909" title="Carpi F.C. 1909">Carpi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> He made his comeback on 13 September during the 1–0 home win against the cross-town rivals of <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a> and opened his scoring account one week later against <a href="/wiki/A.C._Chievo_Verona" class="mw-redirect" title="A.C. Chievo Verona">Chievo Verona</a>, helping Inter to clinch the 4th consecutive victory.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> On 27 September, Icardi was again on the scoresheet but this time in a 1–4 defeat versus <a href="/wiki/ACF_Fiorentina" title="ACF Fiorentina">Fiorentina</a>, who ended Inter's undefeated streak of the 2015–16 season.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>One month later, on 28 October, following the 0–1 away win over <a href="/wiki/Bologna_F.C._1909" title="Bologna F.C. 1909">Bologna</a> where Icardi scored the only goal of the match following an assist from <a href="/wiki/Adem_Ljaji%C4%87" title="Adem Ljaji">Adem Ljaji</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> he complained about lack of services to him, accusing his teammates in the process. Icardi told the media that: "In ten matches I've received four chances to score, and I've taken three. I think that is a good average."<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> After that, he was benched for the following league match against <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">Roma</a>, where Inter won, again a 1–0 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> After the game, coach <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Mancini" title="Roberto Mancini">Mancini</a> said that leaving Icardi on the bench was a "tactical decision", adding that Icardi "must improve his game".<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> He returned to the starting lineup in the next league match against <a href="/wiki/Torino_F.C." title="Torino F.C.">Torino</a>, where Inter grabbed another 1–0 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 22 November, in his 100th <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> appearance, he scored in a 4–0 win over the minnows of <a href="/wiki/Frosinone_Calcio" title="Frosinone Calcio">Frosinone</a>, helping Inter to seal its biggest victory of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> On 13 December, Icardi netted his first brace of the season, in the 0–4 thrashing of <a href="/wiki/Udinese_Calcio" title="Udinese Calcio">Udinese</a>, benefiting in both occasions from the mistakes of Udinese defenders.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> In Inter's final match of 2015, Icardi's goal was not enough to avoid the 2–1 home loss against <a href="/wiki/S.S._Lazio" title="S.S. Lazio">Lazio</a>, but still the team managed to end the year in the first place.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the year, Icardi was ranked the 82nd best footballer in the world by the English newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 6 January 2016, Icardi finished <a href="/wiki/Ivan_Peri%C5%A1i%C4%87" title="Ivan Periši">Ivan Periši</a>'s cross from close range for the only goal away against <a href="/wiki/Empoli_F.C." title="Empoli F.C.">Empoli</a>, putting Inter on top of Serie A.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> A month later, on 3 February, he scored his 50th Inter goal in all competitions in a 1–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/A.C._Chievo_Verona" class="mw-redirect" title="A.C. Chievo Verona">Chievo</a>, returning Inter to its winning ways after four consecutive matches.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> In February 2016, it was reported by several newspapers that Inter had rejected a €30 million bid from <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> to sign Icardi.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> On 9 April, he scored his 50th <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> goal in a 1–0 away win over <a href="/wiki/Frosinone_Calcio" title="Frosinone Calcio">Frosinone</a>, making his 100th Inter appearance in the process.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Icardi started the season on 21 August by playing in the 2–0 away defeat to <a href="/wiki/A.C._Chievo_Verona" class="mw-redirect" title="A.C. Chievo Verona">Chievo</a> in the opening league match,<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> and scored his first goal of the season a week later during the 1–1 draw against <a href="/wiki/U.S._Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Città di Palermo">Palermo</a> at home.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> On 11 September, Icardi scored both goals, including a last-minute winner, as Inter overturn the score against newly promoted side <a href="/wiki/Delfino_Pescara_1936" title="Delfino Pescara 1936">Pescara</a> for the first win of the season under the new coach <a href="/wiki/Frank_de_Boer" title="Frank de Boer">Frank de Boer</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> One week later, in the <a href="/wiki/Derby_d%27Italia" title="Derby d&#39;Italia">Derby d'Italia</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a>, Icardi scored an equalizer in the 68th minute, and provided the <a href="/wiki/Ivan_Peri%C5%A1i%C4%87" title="Ivan Periši">Ivan Periši</a> goal ten minutes later, as Inter overturn the score again to beat the lifetime rivals for the first time in league since November 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> It was Icardi's seventh goal in eight appearances against Juventus, making thus his favourite opponent to score against.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>This was followed by a brace in Inter's 2–0 win at <a href="/wiki/Empoli_F.C." title="Empoli F.C.">Empoli</a> three days later, taking the lead of goalscorers table with six goals in six appearances; it was also the first time that he has scored in four consecutive Serie A matches.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 7 October, Icardi signed a new contract extension with Inter until June 2021, with a buy-out clause of €110 million.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> With the new deal, Icardi will earn €4,5 million per season plus various bonuses based on his performances, goals and image rights. Shortly after signing the contract, Icardi stated: "I'm really happy to have signed this new contract that will keep me at the club until 2021. My dream is to win trophies with this team. I heard lots of things during the transfer window, as you always do, but the club was on my side. I have my agent and wife Wanda to thank for this renewal and we're all pleased at home."<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Icardi scored a brace to beat Torino 2–1 at the San Siro, giving Inter their first win in their last 5 games.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> Then, he continued with his outrageous form, scoring back-to-back home braces against <a href="/wiki/F.C._Crotone" title="F.C. Crotone">Crotone</a> and <a href="/wiki/ACF_Fiorentina" title="ACF Fiorentina">Fiorentina</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> In the last match of 2016, Icardi scored another brace against <a href="/wiki/S.S._Lazio" title="S.S. Lazio">Lazio</a> to help Inter finish the year on a high.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> He finished the first part of the season with 14 goals and 5 assists, being the most efficient striker in top 5 leagues, overtaking stars such <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a> named him the world's 49th best player, winning 33 positions compare to last year ranking.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 15 January 2017, in the 3–1 home win against <a href="/wiki/A.C._Chievo_Verona" class="mw-redirect" title="A.C. Chievo Verona">Chievo</a> which was the fifth consecutive win in league, Icardi scored his 15th league goal of the season becoming the first Inter player to score at least 15 goals in three consecutive seasons since <a href="/wiki/Zlatan_Ibrahimovi%C4%87" title="Zlatan Ibrahimovi">Zlatan Ibrahimovi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Christian_Vieri" title="Christian Vieri">Christian Vieri</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> On 12 March, he scored a hat-trick against Atalanta, bringing his tally to 20 goals for the season.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> Icardi amassed 24 league goals in 34 appearances in the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Inter_Milan_season" title="2016–17 Inter Milan season">2016–17 season</a>, setting a new personal best.<sup id="cite_ref-SW-MI_95-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SW-MI-95">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> In Europa League, he scored twice in five matches as Inter finished last in <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Europa_League_group_stage#Group_K" title="2016–17 UEFA Europa League group stage">Group K</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9319:_Second_Capocannoniere_and_departure"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2017–19:_Second_Capocannoniere_and_departure">2017–19: Second <i>Capocannoniere</i> and departure</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 2017–19: Second Capocannoniere and departure">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:33%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" “ ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" ” ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"He is the captain of Inter, and he is not your average kind of attacker. I have always told that he has the back bone like Ibrahimovic, because he wants the responsibility, he is a special kind of person and football player. A great guy and a great professional."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—Inter manager <a href="/wiki/Luciano_Spalletti" title="Luciano Spalletti">Luciano Spalletti</a>, October 2017<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>Icardi missed much of the <a href="/wiki/Pre-season" class="mw-redirect" title="Pre-season">pre-season</a> after getting injured in May.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> He was ready for the start of the season, however, scoring a brace inside 15 minutes in the opening matchday against Fiorentina as Inter won 3–0.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> He repeated the feat a week later at <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">Roma</a>, as Inter overturned the score to win 3–1,<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> the first league win at <a href="/wiki/Stadio_Olimpico" title="Stadio Olimpico">Stadio Olimpico</a> after nine years; the goals were Icardi's first at the Olimpico as well.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> On 10 September, Icardi scored with penalty kick against <a href="/wiki/S.P.A.L._2013" class="mw-redirect" title="S.P.A.L. 2013">SPAL</a> to record his 76th Serie A goal for <i>Nerazzurri</i>, entering in Inter's top 10 Serie A goalscorers.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later on 15 October, Icardi scored all three goals as Inter defeated cross-town rivals <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a> 3–2 to put Inter in second place.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> He became the first player to score a hat-trick in the <a href="/wiki/Derby_della_Madonnina" title="Derby della Madonnina">Derby della Madonnina</a> since <a href="/wiki/Diego_Milito" title="Diego Milito">Diego Milito</a> in May 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> Later on throughout the season, on 18 March 2018, Icardi scored four goals, including a 14-minute hat-trick, his 6th in Serie A, against his former club, Sampdoria, to give Inter a 5–0 win at the <a href="/wiki/Stadio_Luigi_Ferraris" title="Stadio Luigi Ferraris">Stadio Luigi Ferraris</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> Furthermore, he broke the 100 goal mark in Serie A during the same match, taking his total tally to 103 Serie A goals in his 180th Serie A appearance, becoming the <a href="/wiki/Football_records_in_Italy#Youngest_player_to_score_100_goals_in_Serie_A" class="mw-redirect" title="Football records in Italy">6th youngest player ever to achieve this feat</a>, at the age of 25 years and 27 days; his fourth goal of the match was also his 100th goal for Inter, in his 172nd appearance for the club.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 22 April, Icardi scored a tap-in in the 2–1 away win versus <a href="/wiki/A.C._ChievoVerona" title="A.C. ChievoVerona">Chievo</a> which was his 26th league goal of the season, becoming the first Inter player since <a href="/wiki/Antonio_Valent%C3%ADn_Angelillo" title="Antonio Valentín Angelillo">Angelillo</a> in the 1958–59 season to achieve the feat.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> The next week, Icardi scored on Inter's dramatic 2–3 loss to Juventus, marking his 8th goal in 11 appearances against the Turin side.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the final championship game away versus <a href="/wiki/S.S._Lazio" title="S.S. Lazio">Lazio</a>, Icardi won and converted a penalty kick to temporally level the score in an eventual 3–2 win.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> This win placed Inter fourth in championship tied on points with Lazio but ahead on head-to-head points, meaning the club had returned to Champions League for the first time since 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> With 29 goals, Icardi won the <i><a href="/wiki/Capocannoniere" title="Capocannoniere">Capocannoniere</a></i> jointly with Lazio's <a href="/wiki/Ciro_Immobile" title="Ciro Immobile">Ciro Immobile</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup> breaking his previous record of 24 goals set in the previous season; he also become the first Inter player to reach this tally since <a href="/wiki/Antonio_Angelillo" class="mw-redirect" title="Antonio Angelillo">Antonio Angelillo</a> during the <a href="/wiki/1958%E2%80%9359_Serie_A" title="1958–59 Serie A">1958–59 season</a> (33 goals).
</p><p>Icardi began the new season in slow form, failing to score in the opening six championship matches. He also missed the away game against Bologna due to injury.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> Icardi played his first match in the UEFA Champions League on 18 September in Inter's opening <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage#Group_B" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League group stage">Group B</a> game against <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a>, netting a late equalizer with a 20-yard volley in an eventual 2–1 home win.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> His strike was named Champions League Goal of the Week.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> In the second game away at <a href="/wiki/PSV_Eindhoven" title="PSV Eindhoven">PSV Eindhoven</a>, Icardi was on the score-sheet again by netting a tap-in after taking the ball around goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/Jeroen_Zoet" title="Jeroen Zoet">Jeroen Zoet</a> to give Inter a second 2–1 comeback win.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> By doing so Icardi become the first Inter player since <a href="/wiki/Adriano_(footballer,_born_1982)" title="Adriano (footballer, born 1982)">Adriano</a> in <a href="/wiki/2004%E2%80%9305_Inter_Milan_season" title="2004–05 Inter Milan season">2004–05 season</a> to score in each of his first two Champions League matches.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>By scoring a brace in Inter's 2–1 win at <a href="/wiki/S.P.A.L." title="S.P.A.L.">SPAL</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> Icardi reached 103 Serie A goals by matching <a href="/wiki/Christian_Vieri" title="Christian Vieri">Christian Vieri</a><sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> tally as the seventh player with the most Serie A goals scored with Inter.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup> In the first game following the international break, Icardi played and scored the game-winner against <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a> to make it five league wins in a row for Inter,<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup> also scoring the club's 300th goal in the <a href="/wiki/Derby_della_Madonnina" title="Derby della Madonnina">Derby della Madonnina</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Icardi made his 200th Serie A appearance on 24 November by playing in the last 13 minutes of a 3–0 home win over Frosinone.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup> On 13 February 2019, because of several comments that Icardi's wife, <a href="/wiki/Wanda_Nara" title="Wanda Nara">Wanda Nara</a>, made about Inter's management and its players on the TV program <i>Tiki Taka</i>,<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup> Inter announced that he was to be replaced by <a href="/wiki/Samir_Handanovi%C4%87" title="Samir Handanovi">Samir Handanovi</a> as club captain.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> In response to being stripped of the captaincy, Icardi refused to play in the club's <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">UEFA Europa League</a> match against <a href="/wiki/SK_Rapid_Wien" title="SK Rapid Wien">Rapid Wien</a> the following day.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He returned in action on 3 April in the league match against <a href="/wiki/Genoa_C.F.C." title="Genoa C.F.C.">Genoa</a>, 53 days since his last appearance; on his return, Icardi scored a penalty after being fouled inside the penalty area by <a href="/wiki/Cristian_Romero_(footballer,_born_1998)" title="Cristian Romero (footballer, born 1998)">Cristian Romero</a>, who received a straight red card. In the second half, he also set up Ivan Periši goal before making way for <a href="/wiki/Keita_Balde" class="mw-redirect" title="Keita Balde">Keita Balde</a> in 80th minute.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup> With this goal, Icardi matched Christian Vieri as Inter's eighth all-time top goalscorer with 123 goals.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In July 2019, it was announced that Icardi would not travel on the club's pre-season tour.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup> On 8 August 2019, the club signed Belgian striker <a href="/wiki/Romelu_Lukaku" title="Romelu Lukaku">Romelu Lukaku</a>; the following day he was assigned the number 9 shirt that had been worn by Icardi since his arrival in 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup> To avoid potential legal complications, on 20 August Inter assigned Icardi with the number 7 shirt.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Paris_Saint-Germain">Paris Saint-Germain</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Paris Saint-Germain">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320:_Initial_loan_and_first_trophies"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019–20:_Initial_loan_and_first_trophies">2019–20: Initial loan and first trophies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 2019–20: Initial loan and first trophies">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Mauro_Icardi_(PSG).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Mauro_Icardi_%28PSG%29.jpg/170px-Mauro_Icardi_%28PSG%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="320" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Mauro_Icardi_%28PSG%29.jpg/255px-Mauro_Icardi_%28PSG%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Mauro_Icardi_%28PSG%29.jpg/340px-Mauro_Icardi_%28PSG%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="646" data-file-height="1217" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Mauro_Icardi_(PSG).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Icardi playing for <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> in 2020</div></div></div>
<p>On 2 September 2019, Icardi joined French club <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> on a one-season loan deal with a €70 million option to buy.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> He made his debut for PSG off the bench in their 1–0 win against <a href="/wiki/RC_Strasbourg_Alsace" title="RC Strasbourg Alsace">Strasbourg</a> on 14 September.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup> On 1 October, he scored his first goal for the club in a 1–0 away win over <a href="/wiki/Galatasaray_S.K._(football)" title="Galatasaray S.K. (football)">Galatasaray</a>, in the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2019–20 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup> On 5 October, he scored his first goal in <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Ligue_1" title="2019–20 Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> in a 4–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/Angers_SCO" title="Angers SCO">Angers</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup> Icardi scored a brace against <a href="/wiki/Le_Classique" title="Le Classique">rivals</a> <a href="/wiki/Olympique_de_Marseille" title="Olympique de Marseille">Marseille</a> on 27 October in a 4–0 win.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup> He got his first <a href="/wiki/Hat-trick" title="Hat-trick">hat-trick</a> for the club on 8 January 2020, in a 6–1 <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Coupe_de_la_Ligue" title="2019–20 Coupe de la Ligue">Coupe de la Ligue</a> win over <a href="/wiki/AS_Saint-%C3%89tienne" title="AS Saint-Étienne">Saint-Étienne</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 1 May, Icardi won his first club trophy, as PSG were crowned Ligue 1 champions after the season had been called off amid the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic_in_France" title="COVID-19 pandemic in France">COVID-19 pandemic</a>; at the time of the league's premature suspension, PSG were in first place, with a twelve–point lead over second–placed Marseille.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup> After the season resumed in the summer, Icardi went onto win the <a href="/wiki/Coupe_de_France" title="Coupe de France">Coupe de France</a>, <a href="/wiki/Coupe_de_la_Ligue" title="Coupe de la Ligue">Coupe de la Ligue</a>, and reached the <a href="/wiki/2019-20_UEFA_Champions_League" class="mw-redirect" title="2019-20 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> final, in which he remained an unused substitute despite being the team's leading goalscorer in the tournament with 5 goals in 7 games, alongside <a href="/wiki/Kylian_Mbapp%C3%A9" title="Kylian Mbappé">Kylian Mbappé</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup> On 31 May, Paris Saint-Germain and Inter Milan reached an agreement for Icardi's transfer, worth a reported €60 million.<sup id="cite_ref-PSGBBC_144-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PSGBBC-144">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup> Icardi signed a four-year contract with PSG.<sup id="cite_ref-PSGBBC_144-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PSGBBC-144">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321:_Injury_struggles"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21:_Injury_struggles">2020–21: Injury struggles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 2020–21: Injury struggles">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Icardi missed the first two matches of the season, which were against <a href="/wiki/RC_Lens" title="RC Lens">Lens</a> and <a href="/wiki/Olympique_de_Marseille" title="Olympique de Marseille">Marseille</a>, due to having tested positive for <a href="/wiki/Coronavirus_disease_2019" class="mw-redirect" title="Coronavirus disease 2019">COVID-19</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup> He made his return to action on 16 September 2020, in a 1–0 win against <a href="/wiki/FC_Metz" title="FC Metz">Metz</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup> and scored his first two goals of the season in a 0–2 win against <a href="/wiki/Stade_de_Reims" title="Stade de Reims">Reims</a> on 27 September.<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup> In October 2020, PSG manager <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Tuchel" title="Thomas Tuchel">Thomas Tuchel</a> announced that Icardi had suffered an injury to the internal ligament of the knee.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup> Icardi's return to play came on 28 November, as he came on as a substitute in a 2–2 league draw against <a href="/wiki/FC_Girondins_de_Bordeaux" title="FC Girondins de Bordeaux">Bordeaux</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup> Before the next match against <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a>, he suffered a setback on his injury, and his time on the sidelines was extended.<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup> He had to wait until 9 January 2021 to make his return, coming on as a substitute in a 3–0 win against <a href="/wiki/Stade_Brestois_29" title="Stade Brestois 29">Brest</a>; he would go on to score a goal himself and assist another for <a href="/wiki/Pablo_Sarabia" title="Pablo Sarabia">Pablo Sarabia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup> In the following match, which was against rivals Marseille in the <a href="/wiki/Troph%C3%A9e_des_Champions" title="Trophée des Champions">Trophée des Champions</a>, Icardi scored a goal and won a penalty, as PSG were victorious 2–1. He was awarded the <a href="/wiki/Player_of_the_match" title="Player of the match">man of the match</a> trophy.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Youth">Youth</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Youth">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In April 2012, Icardi received a call-up from <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_under-19_football_team" title="Italy national under-19 football team">Italy under-19</a> squad to play in the friendly against <a href="/wiki/England_national_under-19_football_team" title="England national under-19 football team">England</a>, but the player refused to accept the invitation as he wanted to play for Argentina.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup> His wish was fulfilled on 26 July where he was summoned by <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_under-20_football_team" title="Argentina national under-20 football team">Argentina under-20</a> coach <a href="/wiki/Marcelo_Trobbiani" title="Marcelo Trobbiani">Marcelo Trobbiani</a> to play in the friendly against <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_under-21_football_team" title="Germany national under-21 football team">Germany</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup> in which he made his debut on 14 August at <a href="/wiki/Commerzbank-Arena" class="mw-redirect" title="Commerzbank-Arena">Commerzbank-Arena</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/L%27Alc%C3%BAdia_International_Football_Tournament" title="L&#39;Alcúdia International Football Tournament">L'Alcúdia Tournament</a>, held in Valencia, Spain.
</p><p>Icardi scored his first goal with Argentina U20 on 19 August in a 2–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Japan_national_under-20_football_team" title="Japan national under-20 football team">Japan</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup> which was followed by another two in the 2–1 win against <a href="/wiki/Turkey_national_under-20_football_team" title="Turkey national under-20 football team">Turkey</a> three days later.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup> The tournament ended in conquest, as Icardi was the top scorer with three goals.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Senior">Senior</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Senior">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Following <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italy national football team</a> manager <a href="/wiki/Cesare_Prandelli" title="Cesare Prandelli">Cesare Prandelli</a>'s interest in Icardi's performances, in February 2013, Icardi stated his wish to play for the <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina senior team</a>, despite also being eligible to play for Italy, saying: "I'm very grateful to Italian football for the opportunity it has given me, I'd also like to thank Prandelli for the nice words he expressed about me. But I have to be honest and sincere – I'm Argentine, I feel Argentine, and I've always dreamed of wearing the shirt of my nation. To actually do that would be the maximum for me."<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 15 October 2013, he played his first game for the main squad, coming on as an 82nd-minute substitute for <a href="/wiki/Augusto_Fern%C3%A1ndez" title="Augusto Fernández">Augusto Fernández</a> in a 2–3 <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">FIFA World Cup</a> qualifier loss away to <a href="/wiki/Uruguay_national_football_team" title="Uruguay national football team">Uruguay</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In April 2016, Icardi was excluded from <a href="/wiki/Gerardo_Martino" title="Gerardo Martino">Gerardo Martino</a>'s preliminary squad for the <a href="/wiki/Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_Centenario" title="Copa América Centenario">Copa América Centenario</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup> although the Argentine manager later named him to Argentina's preliminary under-23 squad for the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2016_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Football at the 2016 Summer Olympics – Men&#39;s tournament">2016 Summer Olympics</a> in Rio de Janeiro.<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup> However, Inter did not release Icardi to participate in the Olympics.<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In October 2016, rumours started to speculate in Argentina that <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a> was behind Icardi's exclusion from the national team due to his friendship with <a href="/wiki/Maxi_L%C3%B3pez" title="Maxi López">Maxi López</a>, his wife's former partner.<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup> The national team coach <a href="/wiki/Edgardo_Bauza" title="Edgardo Bauza">Edgardo Bauza</a> stated that Icardi's off-field antics have nothing to do with him not being selected for Argentina and he would receive a call-up soon, adding that Messi does not "dictate" the team.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup> However, he was omitted again for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(CONMEBOL)" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification (CONMEBOL)">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification matches</a> against <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a> and <a href="/wiki/Colombia_national_football_team" title="Colombia national football team">Colombia</a> in November.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 19 May 2017, Icardi received his first call-up after more than three years by newly appointed coach <a href="/wiki/Jorge_Sampaoli" title="Jorge Sampaoli">Jorge Sampaoli</a> for the friendlies against <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a> and <a href="/wiki/Singapore_national_football_team" title="Singapore national football team">Singapore</a> in June.<sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In May 2018, Icardi was named in Argentina's preliminary 35-man <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">squad</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> in <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup> Later that month, however, he was left out from the final 23.<sup id="cite_ref-:3_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:3-9">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Icardi scored his first senior international goal on 20 November 2018, in a 2–0 friendly home win over <a href="/wiki/Mexico_national_football_team" title="Mexico national football team">Mexico</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup> His goal, scored after just 71 seconds, was the fourth quickest goal in Argentina history.<sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup> In this match, he won the first trophy with the senior team - Copa Adidas 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-174" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-174">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In May 2019, Icardi was included in Argentina manager <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Scaloni" title="Lionel Scaloni">Lionel Scaloni</a>'s preliminary 40-man squad for the <a href="/wiki/2019_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2019 Copa América">2019 Copa América</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup> Later that month, however, he was excluded from the final 23-man squad for the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-176" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-176">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:33%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"He chips away at you mentally, in the sense that you have to be concentrated all the time. I’ve only encountered one who is worse for that, but he’s playing with me this year!"</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—<a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italy</a> &amp; <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> defender <a href="/wiki/Giorgio_Chiellini" title="Giorgio Chiellini">Giorgio Chiellini</a>, labelling Icardi as the second toughest opponent he has ever faced.<sup id="cite_ref-177" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-177">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>Nicknamed <i>El niño del partido</i>,<sup id="cite_ref-Chi_è_Mauro_Icardi_178-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Chi_è_Mauro_Icardi-178">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup> Icardi is a quick, tactically intelligent, and physically strong striker, with good technique. Known for his excellent attacking movement, positioning, an eye for goal, he mainly operates in central areas inside the penalty box; an accurate and efficient finisher with his head and either foot inside the area, he is known for his ability to score from few touches, although he can also hold up the ball in order to create space or chances for other players, and play off of his teammates.<sup id="cite_ref-Chi_è_Mauro_Icardi_178-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Chi_è_Mauro_Icardi-178">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Everything_you_need_to_know_about_Chelsea_and_Liverpool_target_Mauro_Icardi_179-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Everything_you_need_to_know_about_Chelsea_and_Liverpool_target_Mauro_Icardi-179">&#91;178&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180">&#91;179&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Internazionale&#39;s_Mauro_Icardi_begins_to_make_right_headlines_in_Fiorentina_win_181-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Internazionale&#39;s_Mauro_Icardi_begins_to_make_right_headlines_in_Fiorentina_win-181">&#91;180&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-182" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-182">&#91;181&#93;</a></sup> Although he was once criticised for his limited creative and defensive contribution, as well as his lack of significant pace, stamina, power, and movement outside the box,<sup id="cite_ref-Everything_you_need_to_know_about_Chelsea_and_Liverpool_target_Mauro_Icardi_179-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Everything_you_need_to_know_about_Chelsea_and_Liverpool_target_Mauro_Icardi-179">&#91;178&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Internazionale&#39;s_Mauro_Icardi_begins_to_make_right_headlines_in_Fiorentina_win_181-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Internazionale&#39;s_Mauro_Icardi_begins_to_make_right_headlines_in_Fiorentina_win-181">&#91;180&#93;</a></sup> his work-rate has improved in recent seasons, and has seen him drift out to wide positions in order to create space or provide assists for teammates.<sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183">&#91;182&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-184" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-184">&#91;183&#93;</a></sup> Long regarded as a talented and promising prospect,<sup id="cite_ref-Everything_you_need_to_know_about_Chelsea_and_Liverpool_target_Mauro_Icardi_179-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Everything_you_need_to_know_about_Chelsea_and_Liverpool_target_Mauro_Icardi-179">&#91;178&#93;</a></sup> in 2013, <a href="/wiki/Don_Bal%C3%B3n" title="Don Balón">Don Balón</a> listed him as one of the top 100 young players born after 1992.<sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185">&#91;184&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Speaking of Icardi, Inter coach <a href="/wiki/Stefano_Pioli" title="Stefano Pioli">Stefano Pioli</a> stated that Icardi "is an animal in the box", and "always finding the right position",<sup id="cite_ref-:0_186-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-186">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup> while the <a href="/wiki/1982_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1982 FIFA World Cup">1982 FIFA World Cup</a> winner <a href="/wiki/Paolo_Rossi" title="Paolo Rossi">Paolo Rossi</a> described Icardi as a "deadly striker", adding that "even in the most complicated games he can create the right opportunity and take advantage of it."<sup id="cite_ref-:1_187-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-187">&#91;186&#93;</a></sup> Inter manager Luciano Spalletti called him "a complete striker" adding that "for his age shoulders so much responsibility".<sup id="cite_ref-188" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-188">&#91;187&#93;</a></sup> In an interview in January 2015, Icardi said his role model is <a href="/wiki/Gabriel_Batistuta" title="Gabriel Batistuta">Gabriel Batistuta</a>, but during his time at Barcelona, he added that the forward he mostly resembled was <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Eto%27o" title="Samuel Eto&#39;o">Samuel Eto'o</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Icardi is married to Argentine media personality <a href="/wiki/Wanda_Nara" title="Wanda Nara">Wanda Nara</a>. Nara was married to Icardi's former <a href="/wiki/U.C._Sampdoria" title="U.C. Sampdoria">Sampdoria</a> teammate <a href="/wiki/Maxi_L%C3%B3pez" title="Maxi López">Maxi López</a>, but the couple split after her relationship with Icardi was exposed. She and López began divorce proceedings in December 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-:4_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:4-10">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Nara and Icardi subsequently married on 27 May 2014, not long after the divorce was finalised, at a small ceremony in <a href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires" title="Buenos Aires">Buenos Aires</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> They have two daughters, Francesca, born on 19 January 2015,<sup id="cite_ref-190" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-190">&#91;189&#93;</a></sup> and Isabella, born on 27 October 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The marriage to Wanda provoked animosity against Icardi in Argentina, making him a target of rumors and unsubstantiated claims by Argentinian tabloids. It has been argued that, arguably, the generalized hatred against him has been an important factor against his being called to the national team, and even prospective calls have been heavily criticized by people like the late  <a href="/wiki/Diego_Maradona" title="Diego Maradona">Diego Maradona</a>, who had entangled in bitter exchanges with Icardi on Twitter as a result of his marriage to Nara.<sup id="cite_ref-:5_192-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:5-192">&#91;191&#93;</a></sup> During an April 2014 <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> match between Sampdoria and Inter, López notably refused to shake Icardi's hand, leading the press to dub the game the "Wanda derby".<sup id="cite_ref-193" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-193">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup> Two years later, López repeated the story by again refusing to shake Icardi's hand during a Serie A match against <a href="/wiki/Torino_F.C." title="Torino F.C.">Torino</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-194" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-194">&#91;193&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Icardi is of <a href="/wiki/Italian_Argentines" title="Italian Argentines">Italian</a> origin through his paternal ancestors named Icardi from <a href="/wiki/Piedmont" title="Piedmont">Piedmont</a> and Da Mezan from <a href="/wiki/Venice" title="Venice">Venice</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-195" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-195">&#91;194&#93;</a></sup> He has an Italian passport.<sup id="cite_ref-196" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-196">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup> He features on the cover of the Italian version of <a href="/wiki/EA_Sports" title="EA Sports">EA Sports</a>' <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA_16" title="FIFA 16">FIFA 16</a></i>, alongside global cover star and compatriot <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-197" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-197">&#91;196&#93;</a></sup> On 6 December 2015, Icardi was robbed of his £29,000 <a href="/wiki/Hublot" title="Hublot">Hublot</a> watch after Inter's 1–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Genoa_CFC" class="mw-redirect" title="Genoa CFC">Genoa</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-198" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-198">&#91;197&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 11 October 2016, Icardi released his autobiography called <i>Sempre Avanti</i> (Always Forward) published by Sperling &amp; Kupfer. The book caused controversy as Icardi had described an incident which offended certain Inter fans, leading to a banner being displayed calling for Icardi to leave the club.<sup id="cite_ref-199" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-199">&#91;198&#93;</a></sup> He was fined by the club and was forced to remove that chapter from the book.<sup id="cite_ref-200" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-200">&#91;199&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-201" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201">&#91;200&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In September 2020 he tested positive for <a href="/wiki/Coronavirus_disease_2019" class="mw-redirect" title="Coronavirus disease 2019">COVID-19</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-202" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-202">&#91;201&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Honours">Honours</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Honours">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_2">Club</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Club">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Individual">Individual</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mauro_Icardi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Individual">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
